5: Backup. </strong></div></h3><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="max-w-3xl w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 page-api-block:ml-0">If you have successfully created a validator, be sure to save your [&amp;&gt;a:hover]:text-yellow-800 [&amp;&gt;code]:bg-yellow-600/5 [&amp;&gt;code]:text-inherit [&amp;&gt;code]:shadow-none text-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-200 dark:[&amp;&gt;a]:text-yellow dark:[&amp;&gt;a:hover]:text-yellow-600 dark:[&amp;&gt;code]:bg-yellow-200/2 dark:[&amp;&gt;code]:text-inherit decoration-yellow-700/6 dark:decoration-yellow/6 flip-heading-hash"></p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="max-w-3xl w-full mx-auto [&amp;&gt;a]:text-yellow-700 [&amp;&gt;a:hover]:text-yellow-800 [&amp;&gt;code]:bg-yellow-600/5 [&amp;&gt;code]:text-inherit [&amp;&gt;code]:shadow-none text-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-200 dark:[&amp;&gt;a]:text-yellow dark:[&amp;&gt;a:hover]:text-yellow-600 dark:[&amp;&gt;code]:bg-yellow-200/2 dark:[&amp;&gt;code]:text-inherit decoration-yellow-700/6 dark:decoration-yellow/6 flip-heading-hash">SAVE YOUR PRIVATE KEY AFTER ENTERING THE COMMAND

The <span class="text-red-500"><strong class="font-bold">priv_validator_key.json</strong></span> is the key with which you can always restore the operation of your validator, so keep it and in case of reinstallation/transfer of the validator to another server - transfer it too.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="max-w-3xl w-full mx-auto [&amp;&gt;a]:text-yellow-700 [&amp;&gt;a:hover]:text-yellow-800 [&amp;&gt;code]:bg-yellow-600/5 [&amp;&gt;code]:text-inherit [&amp;&gt;code]:shadow-none text-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-200 dark:[&amp;&gt;a]:text-yellow dark:[&amp;&gt;a:hover]:text-yellow-600 dark:[&amp;&gt;code]:bg-yellow-200/2 dark:[&amp;&gt;code]:text-inherit decoration-yellow-700/6 dark:decoration-yellow/6 flip-heading-hash">Also remember, if you are a validator with a sufficient number of delegated tokens and you are in an active set, signing blocks, always save <span class="text-red-500"><strong class="font-bold">priv_validator_state.json</strong></span> - this file contains information about the signed blocks of your validators, and in case of restoring the validator after reinstallation or on another server , this file won&#x27;t give you the old blocks again, otherwise you&#x27;ll end up in jail with no way out

💡 Hint:</p><!--/$--><!--$--><ul class="list-none space-y-2 [&amp;&gt;li]:relative [&amp;&gt;li]:ps-[2.25ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-dark/6
